    function v1.hit(p1) --[[ hit | Line: 25 | Upvalues: ClientEvent (copy) ]]

    		if p1.shot_times > 2 then
    			Instance.new("Fire").Parent = p1.instance
    		if p1.shot_times > 3 then
    			p1.destroyed = true
    			p1.instance:Destroy()
    			ClientEvent.emit_event({
    				explosion_effect_type = "barrel",
    				position = p1.barrel.Position
    			})
    function v1.resync_hit(p1) --[[ resync_hit | Line: 43 ]]

    return {
    	ClientExplosiveShootable = v1

  upgrade_profile (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.module.rodux.profile_store.upgrade_profile
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    local RuntimeLib = require(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("include"):WaitForChild("RuntimeLib"))
    local Output = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "class", "Output").Output
    local AssignmentConfig = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "module", "namespace", "AssignmentConfig").AssignmentConfig
    local AttachmentCamoData = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "module", "namespace", "AttachmentCamoData").AttachmentCamoData
    local rename_attachment_code = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "module", "util", "rename_attachment_code").rename_attachment_code
    local function v1(p1, p2) --[[ upgrade_user_data | Line: 7 | Upvalues: Output (copy), AttachmentCamoData (copy), v1 (copy), rename_attachment_code (copy), AssignmentConfig (copy) ]]
    	local v12 = Output.new({ "upgrade_profile", p1 })
    	local profile = p2.profile
    	if profile.version == 16 then
    		return profile
    	elseif profile.version == 15 then
    		return {
    			analytics = {
    				last_match_date = profile.last_match_date,
    				last_played_version = profile.last_played_version
    			},
    			assignments = profile.assignments,
    			claimed_codes = profile.claimed_codes,
    			currency = profile.currency,
    			custom_chat_tag = profile.custom_chat_tag,
    			misc = {
    				is_crayon_available = false
    			},
    			quests = {
    				daily_assignments_deadline = profile.daily_assignments_deadline,
    				free_assignment_rerolls = profile.free_assignment_rerolls,
    				paid_assignment_rerolls = profile.paid_assignment_rerolls
    			},
    			statistics = profile.statistics,
    			viewed_prompts = profile.viewed_prompts
    		}
    	elseif profile.version == 22 then
    		v12:info((("[%*] upgrading chi version profile"):format(p1)))
    		for k, v in pairs(profile.statistics.weapon) do
    			local t = {}
    			for k2, v2 in pairs(v.owned_camo) do
    				local t2 = {}
    					t2[AttachmentCamoData.get_camo_pretty_name(v3)] = true
    				t[k2] = t2
    			v.owned_camo = t
    		profile.version = 15
    		p2.profile = profile
    		return v1(p1, p2)
    	elseif profile.version == 14 then
    		for k, v in pairs(profile.statistics.weapon) do
    			local owned_attachments = v.owned_attachments
    			local v4 = table.create(#owned_attachments)
    			for v5, v6 in owned_attachments do
    				v4[v5] = rename_attachment_code(v6, v5 - 1, owned_attachments)
    			v.owned_attachments = v4
    			for k2, v2 in pairs(v.owned_camo) do
    				local v7 = rename_attachment_code(k2)
    				if v7 ~= k2 then
    					v.owned_camo[v7] = v2
    					v.owned_camo[k2] = nil
    		profile.paid_assignment_rerolls = 0
    		profile.free_assignment_rerolls = AssignmentConfig.free_rerolls_per_day
    		profile.version = 22
    		return v1(p1, p2)
    	elseif profile.version == 11 then
    		profile.statistics.achievements = {
    		}
    		profile.version = 14
    		return v1(p1, p2)
    	elseif profile.version == 10 then
    		v12:info((("[%*] upgrading limo version profile"):format(p1)))
    		profile.version = 11
    		for k, v in pairs(profile.statistics.weapon) do
    			v.attachment_stats = v.attachment_stats or {}
    			v.owned_camo = {}
    		v12:info("granting ownership to existing player camo")
    		return v1(p1, p2)
    	elseif profile.version == 9 then
    		local v9 = table.clone(profile)
    		setmetatable(v9, nil)
    		v9.last_played_version = "0.0.0"
    		v9.version = 10
    		p2.profile = v9
    		return v1(p1, p2)
    	elseif profile.version == 8 then
    		v12:info((("[%*] upgrading india version profile"):format(p1)))
    		local v10 = table.clone(profile)
    		setmetatable(v10, nil)
    		v10.claimed_codes = {}
    		v10.version = 9
    		v10.statistics.player.total_penetration_kills = 0
    		p2.profile = v10
    		return v1(p1, p2)
    	elseif profile.version == 7 then
    		v12:info((("[%*] upgrading hotel version profile"):format(p1)))
    		local v11 = table.clone(profile)
    		setmetatable(v11, nil)
    		v11.claimed_codes = {}
    		v11.version = 8
    		p2.profile = v11
    		return v1(p1, p2)
    	elseif profile.version == 6 then
    		v12:info((("[%*] upgrading golf version profile"):format(p1)))
    		local v122 = table.clone(profile)
    		setmetatable(v122, nil)
    		v122.version = 7
    		v122.viewed_prompts = {}
    		p2.profile = v122
    		return v1(p1, p2)
    	elseif profile.version == 5 then
    		v12:info((("[%*] upgrading foxtrot version profile"):format(p1)))
    		local t = {
    			assignments = {},
    			currency = profile.currency
    		}
    		local t2 = {}
    		local v13 = table.clone(profile.statistics.player)
    		setmetatable(v13, nil)
    		v13.total_explosive_kills = 0

  default_explosive_properties (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.module.data.game.default_explosive_properties
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    local v1 = require(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("include"):WaitForChild("RuntimeLib")).import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "framework", "core", "manifest", "item_manifest").get_weapon("M67")

    	error("M67 is not a throwable weapon")

    }

  default_loadout (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.module.data.game.default_loadout
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    local RuntimeLib = require(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("include"):WaitForChild("RuntimeLib"))
    local v1 = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "include", "node_modules", "@rbxts", "services")
    local DEFAULT_EDITOR_ROOM = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "client", "module", "loadout_room").DEFAULT_EDITOR_ROOM
    local get_weapon = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "framework", "core", "manifest", "item_manifest").get_weapon
    local RuntimeSetupSerialize = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "module", "namespace", "RuntimeSetupSerialize").RuntimeSetupSerialize
    local TestConfig = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "module", "namespace", "TestConfig").TestConfig
    local copy_table = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "module", "util", "lua", "util").copy_table
    local expect = RuntimeLib.import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "module", "util", "ts_util").expect
    local v2 = if v1.RunService:IsRunning() then "M4A1" else TestConfig.get().TEST_WEAPON
    local v3 = expect(get_weapon(v2), "DEFAULT_PRIMARY")
    local v4 = expect(get_weapon("TT33"), "DEFAULT_SECONDARY")
    if not v3.is_customizable then
    	error("DEFAULT_PRIMARY is not customizable")
    if not v4.is_customizable then
    	error("DEFAULT_SECONDARY is not customizable")
    local t = {
    	name = "Default Loadout",
    	primary = {
    		setup = RuntimeSetupSerialize.encode(v3.defaults.default)
    	},
    	secondary = {
    		code = "TT33",
    		setup = RuntimeSetupSerialize.encode(v4.defaults.default)
    	},
    	throwable1 = {
    		code = "F1",
    	},
    	throwable2 = {
    	},
    	uuid = v1.HttpService:GenerateGUID()
    }
    local t2 = {
    	selected_loadout = 0,
    	loadouts = { copy_table(t) },
    	selected_background = DEFAULT_EDITOR_ROOM
